         === app.py ===
         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         from datetime import datetime
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         # Filepaths
         AUCTIONS_FILE = "data/auctions.txt"
         CATEGORIES_FILE = "data/categories.txt"
         BIDS_FILE = "data/bids.txt"
         WINNERS_FILE = "data/winners.txt"
         BID_HISTORY_FILE = "data/bid_history.txt"
         ITEMS_FILE = "data/items.txt"
         TRENDING_FILE = "data/trending.txt"
         
         # Helper functions to load and save data
         
         def load_auctions():
             auctions = []
             if os.path.exists(AUCTIONS_FILE):
                 with open(AUCTIONS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 9:
                             try:
                                 auctions.append({
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'item_name': parts[1],
                                     'description': parts[2],
                                     'category': parts[3],
                                     'starting_bid': float(parts[4]),
                                     'current_bid': float(parts[5]),
                                     'end_time': parts[6],
                                     'status': parts[7],
                                     'image_url': parts[8]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return auctions
         
         def save_auctions(auctions):
             lines = []
             for a in auctions:
                 lines.append('|'.join([
                     str(a['auction_id']),
                     a['item_name'],
                     a['description'],
                     a['category'],
                     f"{a['starting_bid']:.2f}",
                     f"{a['current_bid']:.2f}",
                     a['end_time'],
                     a['status'],
                     a['image_url']
                 ]))
             with open(AUCTIONS_FILE, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 f.write('\n'.join(lines))
         
         
         def load_categories():
             categories = []
             if os.path.exists(CATEGORIES_FILE):
                 with open(CATEGORIES_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 4:
                             try:
                                 categories.append({
                                     'category_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'category_name': parts[1],
                                     'description': parts[2],
                                     'item_count': int(parts[3])
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return categories
         
         def load_bids():
             bids = []
             if os.path.exists(BIDS_FILE):
                 with open(BIDS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 5:
                             try:
                                 bids.append({
                                     'bid_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                     'bidder_name': parts[2],
                                     'bid_amount': float(parts[3]),
                                     'bid_timestamp': parts[4]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return bids
         
         def save_bids(bids):
             lines = []
             for b in bids:
                 lines.append('|'.join([
                     str(b['bid_id']),
                     str(b['auction_id']),
                     b['bidder_name'],
                     f"{b['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                     b['bid_timestamp']
                 ]))
             with open(BIDS_FILE, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 f.write('\n'.join(lines))
         
         def load_winners():
             winners = []
             if os.path.exists(WINNERS_FILE):
                 with open(WINNERS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             try:
                                 winners.append({
                                     'winner_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                     'item_name': parts[2],
                                     'winner_name': parts[3],
                                     'winning_bid': float(parts[4]),
                                     'win_date': parts[5]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return winners
         
         def load_bid_history():
             history = []
             if os.path.exists(BID_HISTORY_FILE):
                 with open(BID_HISTORY_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             try:
                                 history.append({
                                     'history_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                     'auction_name': parts[2],
                                     'bidder_name': parts[3],
                                     'bid_amount': float(parts[4]),
                                     'bid_timestamp': parts[5]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return history
         
         def save_bid_history(history):
             lines = []
             for h in history:
                 lines.append('|'.join([
                     str(h['history_id']),
                     str(h['auction_id']),
                     h['auction_name'],
                     h['bidder_name'],
                     f"{h['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                     h['bid_timestamp']
                 ]))
             with open(BID_HISTORY_FILE, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 f.write('\n'.join(lines))
         
         def load_trending():
             trending = []
             if os.path.exists(TRENDING_FILE):
                 with open(TRENDING_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             try:
                                 trending.append({
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'item_name': parts[1],
                                     'bid_count': int(parts[2]),
                                     'current_bid': float(parts[3]),
                                     'trending_rank': int(parts[4]),
                                     'time_period': parts[5]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return trending
         
         # Routes
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             auctions = load_auctions()
             categories = load_categories()
             trending = load_trending()
         
             featured_auctions = []
             active_auctions = [a for a in auctions if a['status'] == 'Active']
             sorted_active = sorted(active_auctions, key=lambda a: (-a['current_bid'], a['end_time']))
             for a in sorted_active[:3]:
                 featured_auctions.append({
                     'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': a['item_name'],
                     'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': a['end_time']
                 })
         
             trending_auctions = []
             sorted_trending = sorted(trending, key=lambda t: t['trending_rank'])
             for t in sorted_trending[:3]:
                 trending_auctions.append({
                     'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': t['item_name'],
                     'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
                     'bid_count': t['bid_count']
                 })
         
             categories_context = []
             for c in categories:
                 categories_context.append({
                     'category_id': c['category_id'],
                     'category_name': c['category_name'],
                     'item_count': c['item_count']
                 })
         
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_auctions=featured_auctions, trending_auctions=trending_auctions, categories=categories_context)
         
         @app.route('/catalog')
         def auction_catalog():
             auctions = load_auctions()
             categories = load_categories()
         
             auctions_context = []
             for a in auctions:
                 auctions_context.append({
                     'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': a['item_name'],
                     'description': a['description'],
                     'category': a['category'],
                     'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': a['end_time'],
                     'image_url': a['image_url']
                 })
         
             categories_context = []
             for c in categories:
                 categories_context.append({
                     'category_id': c['category_id'],
                     'category_name': c['category_name']
                 })
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=auctions_context, categories=categories_context)
         
         @app.route('/auction/<int:auction_id>')
         def auction_details(auction_id):
             auctions = load_auctions()
             auction = next((a for a in auctions if a['auction_id'] == auction_id), None)
             if auction is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_catalog'))
         
             bid_history_all = load_bid_history()
             bid_history = [
                 {'bidder_name': b['bidder_name'], 'bid_amount': b['bid_amount'], 'bid_timestamp': b['bid_timestamp']}
                 for b in bid_history_all if b['auction_id'] == auction_id
             ]
         
             return render_template('auction_details.html', auction=auction, bid_history=bid_history)
         
         @app.route('/place_bid/<int:auction_id>')
         def place_bid(auction_id):
             auctions = load_auctions()
             auction = next((a for a in auctions if a['auction_id'] == auction_id), None)
             if auction is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_catalog'))
         
             minimum_bid = max(auction['current_bid'], auction['starting_bid']) + 0.01
         
             auction_context = {
                 'auction_id': auction['auction_id'],
                 'item_name': auction['item_name'],
                 'current_bid': auction['current_bid'],
                 'minimum_bid': round(minimum_bid, 2)
             }
             return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction_context)
         
         @app.route('/submit_bid/<int:auction_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def submit_bid(auction_id):
             bidder_name = request.form.get('bidder_name', '').strip()
             bid_amount_str = request.form.get('bid_amount', '').strip()
         
             if not bidder_name or not bid_amount_str:
                 return redirect(url_for('place_bid', auction_id=auction_id))
             try:
                 bid_amount = float(bid_amount_str)
             except ValueError:
                 return redirect(url_for('place_bid', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             auctions = load_auctions()
             auction = next((a for a in auctions if a['auction_id'] == auction_id), None)
             if auction is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_catalog'))
         
             minimum_bid = max(auction['current_bid'], auction['starting_bid']) + 0.01
             if bid_amount < minimum_bid:
                 return redirect(url_for('place_bid', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')
         
             bids = load_bids()
             new_bid_id = max((b['bid_id'] for b in bids), default=0) + 1
             new_bid = {
                 'bid_id': new_bid_id,
                 'auction_id': auction_id,
                 'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                 'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                 'bid_timestamp': now_str
             }
             bids.append(new_bid)
             save_bids(bids)
         
             # Update auction current_bid
             for a in auctions:
                 if a['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                     a['current_bid'] = bid_amount
                     break
             save_auctions(auctions)
         
             # Append to bid history
             bid_history = load_bid_history()
             new_history_id = max((h['history_id'] for h in bid_history), default=0) + 1
             new_history = {
                 'history_id': new_history_id,
                 'auction_id': auction_id,
                 'auction_name': auction['item_name'],
                 'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                 'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                 'bid_timestamp': now_str
             }
             bid_history.append(new_history)
             save_bid_history(bid_history)
         
             return redirect(url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction_id))
         
         @app.route('/bid_history')
         def bid_history():
             bid_history_raw = load_bid_history()
             bids = [
                 {
                     'bid_id': h['history_id'],
                     'auction_name': h['auction_name'],
                     'bidder_name': h['bidder_name'],
                     'bid_amount': h['bid_amount'],
                     'bid_timestamp': h['bid_timestamp']
                 }
                 for h in bid_history_raw
             ]
             auctions_raw = load_auctions()
             auctions = [{'auction_id': a['auction_id'], 'item_name': a['item_name']} for a in auctions_raw]
             return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=bids, auctions=auctions)
         
         @app.route('/categories')
         def categories():
             categories_raw = load_categories()
             categories_context = []
             for c in categories_raw:
                 categories_context.append({
                     'category_id': c['category_id'],
                     'category_name': c['category_name'],
                     'description': c['description'],
                     'item_count': c['item_count']
                 })
             return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories_context)
         
         @app.route('/category/<int:category_id>')
         def category_items(category_id):
             categories = load_categories()
             category_name = None
             for c in categories:
                 if c['category_id'] == category_id:
                     category_name = c['category_name']
                     break
             if category_name is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('categories'))
         
             auctions = load_auctions()
             filtered_auctions = []
             for a in auctions:
                 if a['category'] == category_name:
                     filtered_auctions.append({
                         'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                         'item_name': a['item_name'],
                         'description': a['description'],
                         'category': a['category'],
                         'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
                         'end_time': a['end_time'],
                         'image_url': a['image_url']
                     })
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, category_name=category_name)
         
         @app.route('/winners')
         def winners():
             winners_raw = load_winners()
             winners_context = []
             for w in winners_raw:
                 winners_context.append({
                     'auction_id': w['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': w['item_name'],
                     'winner_name': w['winner_name'],
                     'winning_bid': w['winning_bid'],
                     'win_date': w['win_date']
                 })
             return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_context)
         
         @app.route('/trending')
         def trending_auctions():
             trending_data = load_trending()
             sorted_trending = sorted(trending_data, key=lambda t: t['trending_rank'])
             trending_context = []
             for t in sorted_trending:
                 trending_context.append({
                     'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': t['item_name'],
                     'bid_count': t['bid_count'],
                     'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
                     'trending_rank': t['trending_rank']
                 })
             return render_template('trending.html', trending_auctions=trending_context)
         
         @app.route('/auction_status')
         def auction_status():
             auctions = load_auctions()
             auctions_context = []
             for a in auctions:
                 auctions_context.append({
                     'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': a['item_name'],
                     'status': a['status'],
                     'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': a['end_time']
                 })
             return render_template('auction_status.html', auctions=auctions_context)
         
         @app.route('/refresh_status', methods=['POST'])
         def refresh_status():
             return redirect(url_for('auction_status'))
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

      📄 Before (full content):
         Test app.py backend routes and business logic; write backend_test_report.txt and backend_feedback.txt
         === app.py ===
         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         from datetime import datetime
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         # Filepaths
         AUCTIONS_FILE = "data/auctions.txt"
         CATEGORIES_FILE = "data/categories.txt"
         BIDS_FILE = "data/bids.txt"
         WINNERS_FILE = "data/winners.txt"
         BID_HISTORY_FILE = "data/bid_history.txt"
         ITEMS_FILE = "data/items.txt"
         TRENDING_FILE = "data/trending.txt"
         
         # Helper functions to load and save data
         
         def load_auctions():
             auctions = []
             if os.path.exists(AUCTIONS_FILE):
                 with open(AUCTIONS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 9:
                             try:
                                 auctions.append({
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'item_name': parts[1],
                                     'description': parts[2],
                                     'category': parts[3],
                                     'starting_bid': float(parts[4]),
                                     'current_bid': float(parts[5]),
                                     'end_time': parts[6],
                                     'status': parts[7],
                                     'image_url': parts[8]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return auctions
         
         def save_auctions(auctions):
             lines = []
             for a in auctions:
                 lines.append('|'.join([
                     str(a['auction_id']),
                     a['item_name'],
                     a['description'],
                     a['category'],
                     f"{a['starting_bid']:.2f}",
                     f"{a['current_bid']:.2f}",
                     a['end_time'],
                     a['status'],
                     a['image_url']
                 ]))
             with open(AUCTIONS_FILE, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 f.write('\n'.join(lines))
         
         
         def load_categories():
             categories = []
             if os.path.exists(CATEGORIES_FILE):
                 with open(CATEGORIES_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 4:
                             try:
                                 categories.append({
                                     'category_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'category_name': parts[1],
                                     'description': parts[2],
                                     'item_count': int(parts[3])
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return categories
         
         def load_bids():
             bids = []
             if os.path.exists(BIDS_FILE):
                 with open(BIDS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 5:
                             try:
                                 bids.append({
                                     'bid_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                     'bidder_name': parts[2],
                                     'bid_amount': float(parts[3]),
                                     'bid_timestamp': parts[4]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return bids
         
         def save_bids(bids):
             lines = []
             for b in bids:
                 lines.append('|'.join([
                     str(b['bid_id']),
                     str(b['auction_id']),
                     b['bidder_name'],
                     f"{b['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                     b['bid_timestamp']
                 ]))
             with open(BIDS_FILE, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 f.write('\n'.join(lines))
         
         def load_winners():
             winners = []
             if os.path.exists(WINNERS_FILE):
                 with open(WINNERS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             try:
                                 winners.append({
                                     'winner_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                     'item_name': parts[2],
                                     'winner_name': parts[3],
                                     'winning_bid': float(parts[4]),
                                     'win_date': parts[5]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return winners
         
         def load_bid_history():
             history = []
             if os.path.exists(BID_HISTORY_FILE):
                 with open(BID_HISTORY_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             try:
                                 history.append({
                                     'history_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                     'auction_name': parts[2],
                                     'bidder_name': parts[3],
                                     'bid_amount': float(parts[4]),
                                     'bid_timestamp': parts[5]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return history
         
         def save_bid_history(history):
             lines = []
             for h in history:
                 lines.append('|'.join([
                     str(h['history_id']),
                     str(h['auction_id']),
                     h['auction_name'],
                     h['bidder_name'],
                     f"{h['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                     h['bid_timestamp']
                 ]))
             with open(BID_HISTORY_FILE, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 f.write('\n'.join(lines))
         
         def load_trending():
             trending = []
             if os.path.exists(TRENDING_FILE):
                 with open(TRENDING_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             try:
                                 trending.append({
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'item_name': parts[1],
                                     'bid_count': int(parts[2]),
                                     'current_bid': float(parts[3]),
                                     'trending_rank': int(parts[4]),
                                     'time_period': parts[5]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return trending
         
         # Routes
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             auctions = load_auctions()
             categories = load_categories()
             trending = load_trending()
         
             featured_auctions = []
             active_auctions = [a for a in auctions if a['status'] == 'Active']
             sorted_active = sorted(active_auctions, key=lambda a: (-a['current_bid'], a['end_time']))
             for a in sorted_active[:3]:
                 featured_auctions.append({
                     'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': a['item_name'],
                     'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': a['end_time']
                 })
         
             trending_auctions = []
             sorted_trending = sorted(trending, key=lambda t: t['trending_rank'])
             for t in sorted_trending[:3]:
                 trending_auctions.append({
                     'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': t['item_name'],
                     'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
                     'bid_count': t['bid_count']
                 })
         
             categories_context = []
             for c in categories:
                 categories_context.append({
                     'category_id': c['category_id'],
                     'category_name': c['category_name'],
                     'item_count': c['item_count']
                 })
         
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_auctions=featured_auctions, trending_auctions=trending_auctions, categories=categories_context)
         
         @app.route('/catalog')
         def auction_catalog():
             auctions = load_auctions()
             categories = load_categories()
         
             auctions_context = []
             for a in auctions:
                 auctions_context.append({
                     'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': a['item_name'],
                     'description': a['description'],
                     'category': a['category'],
                     'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': a['end_time'],
                     'image_url': a['image_url']
                 })
         
             categories_context = []
             for c in categories:
                 categories_context.append({
                     'category_id': c['category_id'],
                     'category_name': c['category_name']
                 })
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=auctions_context, categories=categories_context)
         
         @app.route('/auction/<int:auction_id>')
         def auction_details(auction_id):
             auctions = load_auctions()
             auction = next((a for a in auctions if a['auction_id'] == auction_id), None)
             if auction is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_catalog'))
         
             bid_history_all = load_bid_history()
             bid_history = [
                 {'bidder_name': b['bidder_name'], 'bid_amount': b['bid_amount'], 'bid_timestamp': b['bid_timestamp']}
                 for b in bid_history_all if b['auction_id'] == auction_id
             ]
         
             return render_template('auction_details.html', auction=auction, bid_history=bid_history)
         
         @app.route('/place_bid/<int:auction_id>')
         def place_bid(auction_id):
             auctions = load_auctions()
             auction = next((a for a in auctions if a['auction_id'] == auction_id), None)
             if auction is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_catalog'))
         
             minimum_bid = max(auction['current_bid'], auction['starting_bid']) + 0.01
         
             auction_context = {
                 'auction_id': auction['auction_id'],
                 'item_name': auction['item_name'],
                 'current_bid': auction['current_bid'],
                 'minimum_bid': round(minimum_bid, 2)
             }
             return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction_context)
         
         @app.route('/submit_bid/<int:auction_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def submit_bid(auction_id):
             bidder_name = request.form.get('bidder_name', '').strip()
             bid_amount_str = request.form.get('bid_amount', '').strip()
         
             if not bidder_name or not bid_amount_str:
                 return redirect(url_for('place_bid', auction_id=auction_id))
             try:
                 bid_amount = float(bid_amount_str)
             except ValueError:
                 return redirect(url_for('place_bid', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             auctions = load_auctions()
             auction = next((a for a in auctions if a['auction_id'] == auction_id), None)
             if auction is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_catalog'))
         
             minimum_bid = max(auction['current_bid'], auction['starting_bid']) + 0.01
             if bid_amount < minimum_bid:
                 return redirect(url_for('place_bid', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')
         
             bids = load_bids()
             new_bid_id = max((b['bid_id'] for b in bids), default=0) + 1
             new_bid = {
                 'bid_id': new_bid_id,
                 'auction_id': auction_id,
                 'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                 'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                 'bid_timestamp': now_str
             }
             bids.append(new_bid)
             save_bids(bids)
         
             # Update auction current_bid
             for a in auctions:
                 if a['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                     a['current_bid'] = bid_amount
                     break
             save_auctions(auctions)
         
             # Append to bid history
             bid_history = load_bid_history()
             new_history_id = max((h['history_id'] for h in bid_history), default=0) + 1
             new_history = {
                 'history_id': new_history_id,
                 'auction_id': auction_id,
                 'auction_name': auction['item_name'],
                 'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                 'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                 'bid_timestamp': now_str
             }
             bid_history.append(new_history)
             save_bid_history(bid_history)
         
             return redirect(url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction_id))
         
         @app.route('/bid_history')
         def bid_history():
             bid_history_raw = load_bid_history()
             bids = [
                 {
                     'bid_id': h['history_id'],
                     'auction_name': h['auction_name'],
                     'bidder_name': h['bidder_name'],
                     'bid_amount': h['bid_amount'],
                     'bid_timestamp': h['bid_timestamp']
                 }
                 for h in bid_history_raw
             ]
             auctions_raw = load_auctions()
             auctions = [{'auction_id': a['auction_id'], 'item_name': a['item_name']} for a in auctions_raw]
             return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=bids, auctions=auctions)
         
         @app.route('/categories')
         def categories():
             categories_raw = load_categories()
             categories_context = []
             for c in categories_raw:
                 categories_context.append({
                     'category_id': c['category_id'],
                     'category_name': c['category_name'],
                     'description': c['description'],
                     'item_count': c['item_count']
                 })
             return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories_context)
         
         @app.route('/category/<int:category_id>')
         def category_items(category_id):
             categories = load_categories()
             category_name = None
             for c in categories:
                 if c['category_id'] == category_id:
                     category_name = c['category_name']
                     break
             if category_name is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('categories'))
         
             auctions = load_auctions()
             filtered_auctions = []
             for a in auctions:
                 if a['category'] == category_name:
                     filtered_auctions.append({
                         'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                         'item_name': a['item_name'],
                         'description': a['description'],
                         'category': a['category'],
                         'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
                         'end_time': a['end_time'],
                         'image_url': a['image_url']
                     })
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, category_name=category_name)
         
         @app.route('/winners')
         def winners():
             winners_raw = load_winners()
             winners_context = []
             for w in winners_raw:
                 winners_context.append({
                     'auction_id': w['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': w['item_name'],
                     'winner_name': w['winner_name'],
                     'winning_bid': w['winning_bid'],
                     'win_date': w['win_date']
                 })
             return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_context)
         
         @app.route('/trending')
         def trending_auctions():
             trending_data = load_trending()
             sorted_trending = sorted(trending_data, key=lambda t: t['trending_rank'])
             trending_context = []
             for t in sorted_trending:
                 trending_context.append({
                     'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': t['item_name'],
                     'bid_count': t['bid_count'],
                     'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
                     'trending_rank': t['trending_rank']
                 })
             return render_template('trending.html', trending_auctions=trending_context)
         
         @app.route('/auction_status')
         def auction_status():
             auctions = load_auctions()
             auctions_context = []
             for a in auctions:
                 auctions_context.append({
                     'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': a['item_name'],
                     'status': a['status'],
                     'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': a['end_time']
                 })
             return render_template('auction_status.html', auctions=auctions_context)
         
         @app.route('/refresh_status', methods=['POST'])
         def refresh_status():
             return redirect(url_for('auction_status'))
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

      📄 Before (full content):
         Test app.py backend routes and business logic; write backend_test_report.txt and backend_feedback.txt
         === app.py ===
         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request
         import os
         from datetime import datetime
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.config['SECRET_KEY'] = 'dev-secret-key'
         
         # Filepaths
         AUCTIONS_FILE = "data/auctions.txt"
         CATEGORIES_FILE = "data/categories.txt"
         BIDS_FILE = "data/bids.txt"
         WINNERS_FILE = "data/winners.txt"
         BID_HISTORY_FILE = "data/bid_history.txt"
         ITEMS_FILE = "data/items.txt"
         TRENDING_FILE = "data/trending.txt"
         
         # Helper functions to load and save data
         
         def load_auctions():
             auctions = []
             if os.path.exists(AUCTIONS_FILE):
                 with open(AUCTIONS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 9:
                             try:
                                 auctions.append({
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'item_name': parts[1],
                                     'description': parts[2],
                                     'category': parts[3],
                                     'starting_bid': float(parts[4]),
                                     'current_bid': float(parts[5]),
                                     'end_time': parts[6],
                                     'status': parts[7],
                                     'image_url': parts[8]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return auctions
         
         def save_auctions(auctions):
             lines = []
             for a in auctions:
                 lines.append('|'.join([
                     str(a['auction_id']),
                     a['item_name'],
                     a['description'],
                     a['category'],
                     f"{a['starting_bid']:.2f}",
                     f"{a['current_bid']:.2f}",
                     a['end_time'],
                     a['status'],
                     a['image_url']
                 ]))
             with open(AUCTIONS_FILE, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 f.write('\n'.join(lines))
         
         
         def load_categories():
             categories = []
             if os.path.exists(CATEGORIES_FILE):
                 with open(CATEGORIES_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 4:
                             try:
                                 categories.append({
                                     'category_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'category_name': parts[1],
                                     'description': parts[2],
                                     'item_count': int(parts[3])
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return categories
         
         def load_bids():
             bids = []
             if os.path.exists(BIDS_FILE):
                 with open(BIDS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 5:
                             try:
                                 bids.append({
                                     'bid_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                     'bidder_name': parts[2],
                                     'bid_amount': float(parts[3]),
                                     'bid_timestamp': parts[4]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return bids
         
         def save_bids(bids):
             lines = []
             for b in bids:
                 lines.append('|'.join([
                     str(b['bid_id']),
                     str(b['auction_id']),
                     b['bidder_name'],
                     f"{b['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                     b['bid_timestamp']
                 ]))
             with open(BIDS_FILE, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 f.write('\n'.join(lines))
         
         def load_winners():
             winners = []
             if os.path.exists(WINNERS_FILE):
                 with open(WINNERS_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             try:
                                 winners.append({
                                     'winner_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                     'item_name': parts[2],
                                     'winner_name': parts[3],
                                     'winning_bid': float(parts[4]),
                                     'win_date': parts[5]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return winners
         
         def load_bid_history():
             history = []
             if os.path.exists(BID_HISTORY_FILE):
                 with open(BID_HISTORY_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             try:
                                 history.append({
                                     'history_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[1]),
                                     'auction_name': parts[2],
                                     'bidder_name': parts[3],
                                     'bid_amount': float(parts[4]),
                                     'bid_timestamp': parts[5]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return history
         
         def save_bid_history(history):
             lines = []
             for h in history:
                 lines.append('|'.join([
                     str(h['history_id']),
                     str(h['auction_id']),
                     h['auction_name'],
                     h['bidder_name'],
                     f"{h['bid_amount']:.2f}",
                     h['bid_timestamp']
                 ]))
             with open(BID_HISTORY_FILE, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 f.write('\n'.join(lines))
         
         def load_trending():
             trending = []
             if os.path.exists(TRENDING_FILE):
                 with open(TRENDING_FILE, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) == 6:
                             try:
                                 trending.append({
                                     'auction_id': int(parts[0]),
                                     'item_name': parts[1],
                                     'bid_count': int(parts[2]),
                                     'current_bid': float(parts[3]),
                                     'trending_rank': int(parts[4]),
                                     'time_period': parts[5]
                                 })
                             except Exception:
                                 continue
             return trending
         
         # Routes
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             auctions = load_auctions()
             categories = load_categories()
             trending = load_trending()
         
             featured_auctions = []
             active_auctions = [a for a in auctions if a['status'] == 'Active']
             sorted_active = sorted(active_auctions, key=lambda a: (-a['current_bid'], a['end_time']))
             for a in sorted_active[:3]:
                 featured_auctions.append({
                     'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': a['item_name'],
                     'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': a['end_time']
                 })
         
             trending_auctions = []
             sorted_trending = sorted(trending, key=lambda t: t['trending_rank'])
             for t in sorted_trending[:3]:
                 trending_auctions.append({
                     'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': t['item_name'],
                     'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
                     'bid_count': t['bid_count']
                 })
         
             categories_context = []
             for c in categories:
                 categories_context.append({
                     'category_id': c['category_id'],
                     'category_name': c['category_name'],
                     'item_count': c['item_count']
                 })
         
             return render_template('dashboard.html', featured_auctions=featured_auctions, trending_auctions=trending_auctions, categories=categories_context)
         
         @app.route('/catalog')
         def auction_catalog():
             auctions = load_auctions()
             categories = load_categories()
         
             auctions_context = []
             for a in auctions:
                 auctions_context.append({
                     'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': a['item_name'],
                     'description': a['description'],
                     'category': a['category'],
                     'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': a['end_time'],
                     'image_url': a['image_url']
                 })
         
             categories_context = []
             for c in categories:
                 categories_context.append({
                     'category_id': c['category_id'],
                     'category_name': c['category_name']
                 })
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=auctions_context, categories=categories_context)
         
         @app.route('/auction/<int:auction_id>')
         def auction_details(auction_id):
             auctions = load_auctions()
             auction = next((a for a in auctions if a['auction_id'] == auction_id), None)
             if auction is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_catalog'))
         
             bid_history_all = load_bid_history()
             bid_history = [
                 {'bidder_name': b['bidder_name'], 'bid_amount': b['bid_amount'], 'bid_timestamp': b['bid_timestamp']}
                 for b in bid_history_all if b['auction_id'] == auction_id
             ]
         
             return render_template('auction_details.html', auction=auction, bid_history=bid_history)
         
         @app.route('/place_bid/<int:auction_id>')
         def place_bid(auction_id):
             auctions = load_auctions()
             auction = next((a for a in auctions if a['auction_id'] == auction_id), None)
             if auction is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_catalog'))
         
             minimum_bid = max(auction['current_bid'], auction['starting_bid']) + 0.01
         
             auction_context = {
                 'auction_id': auction['auction_id'],
                 'item_name': auction['item_name'],
                 'current_bid': auction['current_bid'],
                 'minimum_bid': round(minimum_bid, 2)
             }
             return render_template('place_bid.html', auction=auction_context)
         
         @app.route('/submit_bid/<int:auction_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def submit_bid(auction_id):
             bidder_name = request.form.get('bidder_name', '').strip()
             bid_amount_str = request.form.get('bid_amount', '').strip()
         
             if not bidder_name or not bid_amount_str:
                 return redirect(url_for('place_bid', auction_id=auction_id))
             try:
                 bid_amount = float(bid_amount_str)
             except ValueError:
                 return redirect(url_for('place_bid', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             auctions = load_auctions()
             auction = next((a for a in auctions if a['auction_id'] == auction_id), None)
             if auction is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('auction_catalog'))
         
             minimum_bid = max(auction['current_bid'], auction['starting_bid']) + 0.01
             if bid_amount < minimum_bid:
                 return redirect(url_for('place_bid', auction_id=auction_id))
         
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')
         
             bids = load_bids()
             new_bid_id = max((b['bid_id'] for b in bids), default=0) + 1
             new_bid = {
                 'bid_id': new_bid_id,
                 'auction_id': auction_id,
                 'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                 'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                 'bid_timestamp': now_str
             }
             bids.append(new_bid)
             save_bids(bids)
         
             # Update auction current_bid
             for a in auctions:
                 if a['auction_id'] == auction_id:
                     a['current_bid'] = bid_amount
                     break
             save_auctions(auctions)
         
             # Append to bid history
             bid_history = load_bid_history()
             new_history_id = max((h['history_id'] for h in bid_history), default=0) + 1
             new_history = {
                 'history_id': new_history_id,
                 'auction_id': auction_id,
                 'auction_name': auction['item_name'],
                 'bidder_name': bidder_name,
                 'bid_amount': bid_amount,
                 'bid_timestamp': now_str
             }
             bid_history.append(new_history)
             save_bid_history(bid_history)
         
             return redirect(url_for('auction_details', auction_id=auction_id))
         
         @app.route('/bid_history')
         def bid_history():
             bid_history_raw = load_bid_history()
             bids = [
                 {
                     'bid_id': h['history_id'],
                     'auction_name': h['auction_name'],
                     'bidder_name': h['bidder_name'],
                     'bid_amount': h['bid_amount'],
                     'bid_timestamp': h['bid_timestamp']
                 }
                 for h in bid_history_raw
             ]
             auctions_raw = load_auctions()
             auctions = [{'auction_id': a['auction_id'], 'item_name': a['item_name']} for a in auctions_raw]
             return render_template('bid_history.html', bids=bids, auctions=auctions)
         
         @app.route('/categories')
         def categories():
             categories_raw = load_categories()
             categories_context = []
             for c in categories_raw:
                 categories_context.append({
                     'category_id': c['category_id'],
                     'category_name': c['category_name'],
                     'description': c['description'],
                     'item_count': c['item_count']
                 })
             return render_template('categories.html', categories=categories_context)
         
         @app.route('/category/<int:category_id>')
         def category_items(category_id):
             categories = load_categories()
             category_name = None
             for c in categories:
                 if c['category_id'] == category_id:
                     category_name = c['category_name']
                     break
             if category_name is None:
                 return redirect(url_for('categories'))
         
             auctions = load_auctions()
             filtered_auctions = []
             for a in auctions:
                 if a['category'] == category_name:
                     filtered_auctions.append({
                         'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                         'item_name': a['item_name'],
                         'description': a['description'],
                         'category': a['category'],
                         'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
                         'end_time': a['end_time'],
                         'image_url': a['image_url']
                     })
         
             return render_template('catalog.html', auctions=filtered_auctions, category_name=category_name)
         
         @app.route('/winners')
         def winners():
             winners_raw = load_winners()
             winners_context = []
             for w in winners_raw:
                 winners_context.append({
                     'auction_id': w['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': w['item_name'],
                     'winner_name': w['winner_name'],
                     'winning_bid': w['winning_bid'],
                     'win_date': w['win_date']
                 })
             return render_template('winners.html', winners=winners_context)
         
         @app.route('/trending')
         def trending_auctions():
             trending_data = load_trending()
             sorted_trending = sorted(trending_data, key=lambda t: t['trending_rank'])
             trending_context = []
             for t in sorted_trending:
                 trending_context.append({
                     'auction_id': t['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': t['item_name'],
                     'bid_count': t['bid_count'],
                     'current_bid': t['current_bid'],
                     'trending_rank': t['trending_rank']
                 })
             return render_template('trending.html', trending_auctions=trending_context)
         
         @app.route('/auction_status')
         def auction_status():
             auctions = load_auctions()
             auctions_context = []
             for a in auctions:
                 auctions_context.append({
                     'auction_id': a['auction_id'],
                     'item_name': a['item_name'],
                     'status': a['status'],
                     'current_bid': a['current_bid'],
                     'end_time': a['end_time']
                 })
             return render_template('auction_status.html', auctions=auctions_context)
         
         @app.route('/refresh_status', methods=['POST'])
         def refresh_status():
             return redirect(url_for('auction_status'))
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True, port=5000)

         === app.py ===
         from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, flash
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'some_secret_key'
         
         data_dir = 'data'
         
         def load_auctions():
             auctions = []
             filepath = os.path.join(data_dir, 'auctions.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return auctions
             with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     parts = line.strip().split('|')
                     if len(parts) != 6:
                         continue
                     try:
                         auction = {
                             'id': parts[0],
                             'title': parts[1],
                             'category': parts[2],
                             'status': parts[3],  # expected: 'active', 'closed', etc.
                             'starting_price': float(parts[4]),
                             'current_price': float(parts[5])
                         }
                         auctions.append(auction)
                     except ValueError:
                         continue
             return auctions
         
         def save_auctions(auctions):
             filepath = os.path.join(data_dir, 'auctions.txt')
             with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for auction in auctions:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         auction['id'],
                         auction['title'],
                         auction['category'],
                         auction['status'],
                         f"{auction['starting_price']:.2f}",
                         f"{auction['current_price']:.2f}"
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         def load_categories():
             categories = []
             filepath = os.path.join(data_dir, 'categories.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return categories
             with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     parts = line.strip().split('|')
                     if len(parts) < 2:
                         continue
                     category = {
                         'id': parts[0],
                         'name': parts[1]
                     }
                     categories.append(category)
             return categories
         
         def load_trending():
             trending = []
             filepath = os.path.join(data_dir, 'trending.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return trending
             with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     parts = line.strip().split('|')
                     if len(parts) < 2:
                         continue
                     try:
                         item = {
                             'id': parts[0],
                             'rank': int(parts[1]),
                             'title': parts[2] if len(parts) > 2 else ''
                         }
                         trending.append(item)
                     except ValueError:
                         continue
             trending.sort(key=lambda x: x['rank'])
             return trending
         
         @app.route('/')
         def index():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             auctions = load_auctions()
             categories = load_categories()
             trending = load_trending()
         
             featured_auctions = [a for a in auctions if a['status'] == 'active']
             featured_auctions.sort(key=lambda x: x['current_price'], reverse=True)
         
             return render_template('dashboard.html',
                                    featured_auctions=featured_auctions,
                                    categories=categories,
                                    trending=trending)
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)
